            <b>
             TrustedServer technology
            </b>
            guarantees that every ExpressVPN server always loads the exact same secure, up-to-date software, greatly reducing security risks. TrustedServer also allows ExpressVPN servers to operate using only RAM. Because the servers never write to the hard drive,
            <b>
             it is impossible for any data to be stored on the server after a reboot—even accidentally.
            </b>

           <h3>
            Why You Need a VPN
           </h3>
           <p>
            Online dangers are taking your freedom and choice:
           </p>
           <ul>
            <li>
             Cybercriminals are always on the hunt for your personal details so they can
             <b>
              steal your money or even your identity
             </b>
             , using more advanced tools
            </li>
            <li>
             Companies are
             <b>
              tracking you and reaching into your wallet
             </b>
             with dynamic pricing that suits them, while the cheaper prices are kept hidden
            </li>
            <li>
             ISPs are
             <b>
              slowing down your connection
             </b>
             speed when you want to run torrents
            </li>
            <li>
             Governments are
             <b>
              censoring what you can or can not see online
             </b>
            </li>
           </ul>
           <p>
            A VPN is a valuable tool for protecting yourself and taking back your Internet freedom. It allows you to:
           </p>
           <ul>
            <li>
             Enjoy the complete catalogs of Netflix and other streaming services, going around the companies’ movie and series limited-access policies, so you get full value for your subscription
            </li>
            <li>
             Protect your personal data so that it doesn’t fall into the hands of hackers, advertisers, or other third parties
            </li>
            <li>
             Get complete anonymity every time you go online, whether you’re catching up on the news, torrenting files, shopping, or doing research
            </li>
            <li>
             Increase your connection speeds, especially if your ISP is currently throttling it
            </li>
           </ul>
           <p>
            During our most recent tests, we found that there are
            <b>
             over 300 VPN services available
            </b>
            . While many of them can do some of the above—and plenty promise to, just to fall flat—
            <b>
             only the best VPNs can do it all
            </b>
            .
           </p>
           <h2 class="js-tocItem" id="how">
            Research Methodology: How We Ranked &amp; Compared These VPNs
           </h2>
           <p>
            With hundreds of VPNs all claiming to be the best, how do you choose the right one? Well, we’ve done the hard work for you. We’ve tested over 300 of them and compiled the very best VPNs here. Our in-depth reviews give you all the information you need, covering all the important criteria you need to make the right choice.
           </p>
           <p>
            My rigorous tests included many trials, and each of the 300 VPNs I tested were analyzed bit by bit. My research also includes field tests by our researchers in over 30 countries who tested every VPN against local geoblocks, ISPs, government censorship, and tracking. All tests are done periodically to make sure the results you see here are current. Here are the key factors in determining each VPN’s rankings:
           </p>
           <h3>
            Security
           </h3>
           <p>
            Two crucial aspects of a top VPN are
            <b>
             privacy
            </b>
            and
            <b>
             security.
            </b>
            You’ll be hard-pressed to find a provider that doesn’t offer them on paper
            <b>
             —but things can be different in reality.
            </b>
           </p>
           <p>
            A
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/best-no-log-vpns/" target="_blank">
             VPN with a verified no-logs policy
            </a>
            ensures that your digital footprint is secure.
            <b>
             No-logs policies mean none of your data is collected, stored, or shared
            </b>
            while you’re browsing. It protects you from prying eyes and preserves your privacy, making it one of the leading criteria in our VPN rankings.
           </p>
           <h3>
            Speed
           </h3>
           <p>
            Another must-have ingredient in the recipe for the best VPN is
            <b>
             speed.
            </b>
            Using a VPN means your traffic is sent through additional servers, affecting your speed. Every VPN will slow you down in some way; the real question is by how much. The
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/the-fastest-vpns-we-actually-tested-them/" target="_blank">
             fastest VPN services
            </a>
            have
            <b>
             the smallest impact on your connection quality.
            </b>
            They’ll let you browse, torrent, and stream without annoying lag or buffering.
           </p>
           <p>
            A really fast VPN can also help you overcome ISP throttling. You may end up with faster speeds than you started with.
           </p>
           <p>
            Our tests included remote intercontinental connections with limited bandwidth to offer a real challenge to each VPN.
           </p>
           <h3>
            Streaming
           </h3>
           <p>
            Speaking of
            <b>
             streaming,
            </b>
            VPNs are a popular solution for accessing the full range of content on platforms like
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/5-best-vpns-netflix-actually-work/" target="_blank">
             Netflix
            </a>
            <b>
             ,
            </b>
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/5-best-vpns-hulu-actually-work/" target="_blank">
             Hulu
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/5-best-vpns-bbc-iplayer-actually-work/" target="_blank">
             BBC iPlayer
            </a>
            <b>
             ,
            </b>
            and
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/which-vpns-can-actually-access-dazn/" target="_blank">
             DAZN
            </a>
            <b>
             .
            </b>
            <b>
             Such platforms limit their service
            </b>
            depending on your region, but connecting to the right VPN server can open the door to your favorite shows.
           </p>
           <h3>
            Torrenting
           </h3>
           <p>
            VPNs are also useful for torrenting fans—especially in countries where torrents are prohibited. Even if you follow the rules (we recommend you do),
            <b>
             torrenting without extra protection can expose you
            </b>
            to greedy copyright trolls and hackers
            <b>
             .
            </b>
           </p>
           <p>
            P2P connections aren’t secure,
            <b>
             but you can change that
            </b>
            with a
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/best-vpns-for-utorrent-fastest-safest-cheapest/" target="_blank">
             good VPN for torrenting
            </a>
            . By
            <b>
             masking your real IP address and hiding your traffic behind a layer of encryption,
            </b>
            you’ll avoid all the threats that come with downloading torrents while enjoying the benefits. In our VPN comparison, we checked out torrenting features like
            <b>
             P2P profiles, SOCKS5 proxies, and easy setup
            </b>
            with torrent clients.
           </p>
           <h3>
            Censorship
           </h3>
           <p>
            Last but not least, let’s talk
            <b>
             censorship.
            </b>
            You know you’ve landed on a reliable provider when your VPN works in a country that actively tries to block it
            <b>
             .
            </b>
            During our research, we looked at
            <b>
             special features
            </b>
            <b>
             and settings for extra obfuscation.
            </b>
            The top VPN services in our overall list have proven themselves in
            <b>
             censorship-heavy regions
            </b>
            like
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/best-vpns-for-china-verified-list/" target="_blank">
             China
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/best-vpns-for-iran/" target="_blank">
             Iran
            </a>
            , and
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/best-vpns-dubai/" target="_blank">
             the UAE
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Many other factors played a significant part in our final rankings. These include
            <b>
             server network size, encryption, security features, ease of use,
            </b>
            and of course
            <b>
             —price.
            </b>
            We spared no expense in exploring every detail for our VPN reviews and tests.
           </p>
           <h2 class="js-tocItem" id="faqs">
            FAQs
           </h2>
           <h3>
            <span data-faq-question="0">
            </span>
            😀 Are VPNs legal?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="0">
            </span>
            People sometimes think that VPNs may be illegal because they’re occasionally used for illicit purposes. However, in most countries around the world,
            <b>
             VPN use is completely legal
            </b>
            —though
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/are-vpns-legal/" target="_blank">
             there are important exceptions
            </a>
            you need to know about. The only countries where using a VPN is a grey area (and in some cases, forbidden) are China, Iraq, Iran, Russia, Belarus, Turkey, Oman, and the UAE.
           </p>
           <p>
            Those things that a VPN does—
            <b>
             encrypting data, combatting geoblocks, and providing anonymity
            </b>
            —are not illegal. But remember: Anything you do that’s illegal without a VPN is still illegal with a VPN. We do not condone using a VPN for any illegal activities.
           </p>
           <h3>
            <span data-faq-question="1">
            </span>
            😄 Are VPNs safe?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="1">
            </span>
            <b>
             VPNs are safe to use in most countries.
            </b>
            However, it’s your responsibility to make sure you follow the rules and stay out of trouble.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, you may be taking a risk if:
           </p>
           <ul>
            <li>
             You use a non-government-permitted VPN in a country where the government mandates which VPNs are allowed.
            </li>
            <li>
             You torrent copyrighted material with a VPN that
             <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/best-no-log-vpns/" target="_blank">
              keeps logs
             </a>
             or doesn’t have a
             <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/kill-switch-features/" target="_blank">
              kill switch.
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
           <h3>
            <span data-faq-question="2">
            </span>
            🙂 Are VPNs hard to use?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="2">
            </span>
            The best VPNs are
            <b>
             very easy to use
            </b>
            . In most cases, you just need to download the appropriate app for your device, install, and launch.
           </p>
           <p>
            The top VPN services we’ve recommended above have
            <b>
             user-friendly interfaces
            </b>
            that even beginners can easily figure out. Lots of times, you can use a
            <b>
             quick-connect button
            </b>
            to instantly connect to a nearby server. If you’re trying to get around a geoblock, just choose a server in the location of your choice.
           </p>
           <p>
            Tip: If you’re new to VPNs and want to learn more about what they do, check out our
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/vpns-101-vpnmentors-vpn-guide-newbies/" target="_blank">
             VPN guide for newbies
            </a>
            —it’s packed with info about VPN features, uses, and benefits.
           </p>
           <h3>
            <span data-faq-question="3">
            </span>
            😊 How much does a VPN cost?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="3">
            </span>
            After hearing about all the wonderful things that VPNs can do, you might wonder what kind of price tag they come with. All the VPNs I’ve recommended above are
            <b>
             extremely affordable
            </b>
            , with some costing less than $2 per month.
           </p>
           <p>
            Even our top recommendation—
            <a class="shortcode_affiliate_link_41357 aff-link aff-top-vendor" href="https://www.vpnmentor.com?Track_link=NDEzNTd8&amp;vid=41357&amp;target=ShortCodeAffiliateLink_138109_best_vpns_category_42&amp;pageid=138109&amp;type=best_vpns_category" onclick="clickedLinkExternal('Article ? - ShortCode Link ', 'NordVPN');" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
             <b>
              the powerful but affordable NordVPN
             </b>
            </a>
            —is available for less than $4 per month.
           </p>
           <p>
            If you’re ready to make a purchase, first head to our
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/coupons/" target="_blank">
             VPN coupons page
            </a>
            . You’ll find exclusive discounts that will
            <b>
             save you money
            </b>
            .
           </p>
           <h3>
            <span data-faq-question="4">
            </span>
            🤗 Are there free VPNs?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="4">
            </span>
            There are free VPNs available, but our advice is simple:
            <b>
             It’s best to stay away
            </b>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Getting something for nothing is enticing, no doubt. However, with the wrong free VPN, you might pay nothing upfront—but
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/free-vpns-are-not-safe-to-use/" target="_blank">
             you may pay later
            </a>
            in the form of ridiculously slow connection speeds, a malware infection, or even a stolen identity.
           </p>
           <p>
            Not all free VPNs are scams. We recently researched dozens of services to find those
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/top-really-free-vpn-services/" target="_blank">
             free VPNs that truly are legit
            </a>
            . They all come with limitations, such as data caps or restricted access to features, but they’re safe to use if you really need them.
           </p>
           <h3 id="proxy">
            <span data-faq-question="5">
            </span>
            🙂 Can I Use Tor or a Proxy Instead of a VPN?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="5">
            </span>
            Tor, proxies, and VPNs are three completely different types of software that sometimes serve the same use. Let’s take a closer look.
           </p>
           <p>
            <b>
             Tor
            </b>
            (short for
            <b>
             The Onion Router
            </b>
            ) utilizes an anonymizing network that bounces your connection through several volunteer servers. While this process
            <b>
             makes you (and your data) much harder to track,
            </b>
            it will slow you down. Tor is a very complex topic, so check out our
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/tor-browser-work-relate-using-vpn/" target="_blank">
             ultimate guide to Tor
            </a>
            if you’re curious for more info and tips.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/tor-vs-vpn/" target="_blank">
             Compared to VPNs, Tor has its drawbacks.
            </a>
            While it’s free to use, it provides weaker encryption and slower connections. The best move is to
            <b>
             use both Tor and a VPN together
            </b>
            and reap all the benefits. A stable VPN removes Tor’s weaknesses, while Tor improves your privacy even further.
           </p>
           <p>
            That said,
            <b>
             not all VPNs are compatible with Tor.
            </b>
            To make it work, you need a VPN like
            <a class="shortcode_affiliate_link_41357 aff-link aff-top-vendor" href="https://www.vpnmentor.com?Track_link=NDEzNTd8&amp;vid=41357&amp;target=ShortCodeAffiliateLink_138109_best_vpns_category_43&amp;pageid=138109&amp;type=best_vpns_category" onclick="clickedLinkExternal('Article ? - ShortCode Link ', 'NordVPN');" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
             <b>
              NordVPN
             </b>
            </a>
            which offers
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/the-best-vpns-for-tor/" target="_blank">
             specialized Tor over VPN servers
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/proxies-vs-vpn-understanding-the-difference/" target="_blank">
             Proxy services have one advantage over VPNs
            </a>
            : they offer fast speeds (and hide your IP address). However, they have no other security features, don’t encrypt your data, and don’t even offer an interface.
           </p>
           <p>
            <b>
             These features mean proxies are not secure or easy to use.
            </b>
            However, they can improve your connection speeds if privacy isn’t a concern for you.
           </p>
           <p>
            There are hundreds of proxies out there,
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/blog/top-proxy-services/" target="_blank">
             so it’s important to choose the right one
            </a>
            . Better yet,
            <b>
             invest in a fast, cheap VPN
            </b>
            and benefit from extra protection and privacy on top of great speeds.
           </p>
           <p>
            <b>
             Note
            </b>
            : We at vpnMentor provide a
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/proxy/" target="_blank">
             free proxy tool
            </a>
            ! Feel free to use it if you’re in a hurry and don’t have time to pick and choose.
           </p>

            <span data-faq-question="6">
            </span>
            😃 Should I use a VPN on my phone?
           </h3>
           <p>
            <span data-faq-answer="6">
            </span>
            Ideally, you should use a VPN on every internet-enable device you use. After all, every connection to the internet is an opportunity for hacking, surveillance, and tracking.
            <br/>
            Many VPNs, including all the services that make up our best VPNs list above, offer apps for a variety of devices, including smartphones. Would you like to know more? Check out our
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/bestvpns/android/" target="_blank">
             best VPNs for Android
            </a>
            and
            <a href="https://www.vpnmentor.com/bestvpns/ios/" target="_blank">
             best VPNs for iOS
            </a>
            research articles.
           </p>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function QueryStringParse(query) {
    // This function is anonymous, is executed immediately and
    // the return value is assigned to QueryString!
    var query_string = {};
    var vars = query.split("&");
    for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
      var pair = vars[i].split("=");
          // If first entry with this name
      if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "undefined") {
        query_string[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1]);
          // If second entry with this name
      } else if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "string") {
        var arr = [ query_string[pair[0]],decodeURIComponent(pair[1]) ];
        query_string[pair[0]] = arr;
          // If third or later entry with this name
      } else {
        query_string[pair[0]].push(decodeURIComponent(pair[1]));
      }
    }
    return query_string;
}

function issetCookie( key ) {
    if (getCookie(key) != null && typeof getCookie(key) != 'undefined') {
        return true;
    } else {
        return false;
    }
}

function linksTrackingInit(){
   window.trakingLinks = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="Track_link"]');
}

function setTracking( trakingLinks = '') {

    if( trakingLinks === '' ) {
        trakingLinks = window.trakingLinks;
    }

    var bcData = false;
    if ( issetCookie('BC') && getCookie('BC') == 'true') {
        bcData = getCookie('BC');
    }
    trakingLinks.forEach(element => {

        var href = element.getAttribute('href');

        if (href.indexOf('mailto') !== -1){
            return element;
        }

        if(bcData !== false) {
            href = setBcTralingToLink(element, href, bcData);
        }

        href =  aloomaTrackingLink(element, href);

        element.setAttribute('href', href)

    });

}

function setBcTralingToLink(element, href, bcData) {

    if ( element.getAttribute("data-BC-tracked") ) {
        return href;
    }

    element.setAttribute("data-BC-tracked", "yes");

    var arrUrlData = QueryStringParse(href);

    arrUrlData.bc = bcData;

    return Object.getOwnPropertyNames(arrUrlData).map( function (k) {
        return [k, arrUrlData[k]].join('=')
    }).join('&');

}

function aloomaTrackingLink ( element, href )  {

        if ( element.getAttribute("data-tracked") ) {
            return href;
        }

        element.setAttribute("data-tracked", "yes");

        element.setAttribute("target", "_blank");


        var rndClick = (Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 5)).toUpperCase();
        var onClickString = element.getAttribute("onclick");
        var myRegexp = /clickedLinkExternal\(\s*['|"](.*?)['|"]\s*,\s*['|"](.*?)['|"]\s*\)/g;
        var clickoutData = myRegexp.exec(onClickString);

        if(clickoutData == null){
            myRegexp = /clickedLinkExternal\(\s*['|"](.*?)['|"]\s*,\s*['|"](.*?)['|"]\s*,\s*(.*?)\s*\)/g;
            clickoutData = myRegexp.exec(onClickString);
        }
        var vendorName = 'Js Error';
        var btnName = 'Js Error';

        if(clickoutData) {
            vendorName = clickoutData[2];
            btnName = clickoutData[1];
        }

        if( vendorName == 'Js Error' ) {
            var regExpTrackLink = /Track_link=([\w]*)&?/g;
            var TrackLink = regExpTrackLink.exec(href);
            vendorName = atob(TrackLink[1]);
            vendorName = vendorName.substring(0,vendorName.length - 1);
            // console.log(vendorName);
        }

        var regExpTarget = /target=([\w]*)&?/g;
        var targetBtn = regExpTarget.exec(href);

        if(targetBtn) {
            btnName = targetBtn[1];
        }

        // Check is the outong link has "pos" in it, if it is, send's it to Alooma
        var pos = "";
        var posRegexp = /pos=(\d*)/g;
        var posNum = posRegexp.exec(href);
        if (posNum){
            pos=posNum[1];
        }

        // Check is the outong link has "dl" in it, if it is, send's it to Alooma
        var deeplink = "";
        var posRegexp = /dl=(\w*)/g;
        var posNum = posRegexp.exec(href);
        if (posNum){
            deeplink=posNum[1];
        }


        // Check is the outong link has "vid" in it, if it is, send's it to Alooma
        var vid = "";
        var posRegexp = /vid=(\w*)/g;
        var posNum = posRegexp.exec(href);
        if (posNum){
            vid=posNum[1];
        }

        var aloomaClickData = {
            "pageview_id": rndPage,
            "clickout_id" : rndClick,
            "vendor" : vendorName,
            "vendor_id" : vid,
            "btnName" : btnName,
            "pos"   : pos,
            "deeplink": deeplink,
            "current_url" :window.location.href,
            "internalurl" : href
        }

        aloomaClickData.splitCurrentUrl = {};
        aloomaClickData.splitCurrentUrl.host=window.location.origin + window.location.pathname;
        aloomaClickData.splitCurrentUrl.params=TrackingQueryString;

        element.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
            // Middle Button
            console.log( e.which );
            if (e.which === 2) {
                aloomaClickData.mouse_button = "middle";
                aloomaTrackPageview("clickout", aloomaClickData)
                delete aloomaClickData.mouse_button;
                // Emulate clickedLinkExternal() call
                if ( e.currentTarget.onclick ) {
                    window.vmClickMouseButton = "middle";
                    e.currentTarget.onclick(e);
                }
            } else {
                aloomaTrackPageview("clickout", aloomaClickData)
            }
        } );

        element.addEventListener('auxclick', function (e) {
            // Middle Button
            console.log( e.which );
            if (e.which === 2) {
                aloomaClickData.mouse_button = "middle";
                aloomaTrackPageview("clickout", aloomaClickData)
                delete aloomaClickData.mouse_button;
                // Emulate clickedLinkExternal() call
                if ( e.currentTarget.onclick ) {
                    window.vmClickMouseButton = "middle";
                    e.currentTarget.onclick(e);
                }
            } else {
                aloomaTrackPageview("clickout", aloomaClickData)
            }
        } );

        return href + "&clickout_id="+rndClick+"&pageview_id="+rndPage;

}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

    setTimeout(function(){ linksTrackingInit() }, 0);
    setTimeout(function(){ setTracking()  }, 0);
});

/**
 * @param {string} trackType
 * @param {Object} trackData
 * @param redirectUrl
 */
function aloomaTrackPageview(trackType, trackData, redirectUrl, send_pixel) {

     /* add new pixel data */
    if (typeof send_pixel === "undefined") {
        var pixel_img = document.createElement("img");
        pixel_img.setAttribute("src", "https://d3bch4rrbnbe5n.cloudfront.net/pxl.png?data="+encodeURIComponent(b64EncodeUnicode(JSON.stringify(trackData))));
        pixel_img.setAttribute("height", "1");
        pixel_img.setAttribute("width", "1");
        pixel_img.setAttribute("alt", "vpnMentor");
        document.body.appendChild(pixel_img);
    }


	if (typeof alooma !== 'undefined' && alooma.newiknowlogy.track) {
        trackData.event = trackType;


		trackData['verbose'] = true;

		if (typeof window.chosenVariation !== 'undefined'){
			trackData['chosenVariation'] = window.chosenVariation;
        }

		//console.log(trackData);
		if(redirectUrl){
			window.alooma.newiknowlogy.track(
                trackType, trackData, function(responce) { aloomaCallbackError(responce,trackType, trackData, redirectUrl );}
            );
		} else {
			window.alooma.newiknowlogy.track(
                trackType, trackData, function(responce) {aloomaCallbackError(responce,trackType, trackData );}
            );
		}

        window.aloomaEvents = window.aloomaEvents || [];

        window.aloomaEvents.push( {
            "name" : trackType,
            "data" : trackData
        } )

    } else {
		setTimeout(function() {
    		aloomaTrackPageview(trackType, trackData, redirectUrl, false);
        }, 50);
    }
}

function aloomaCallbackError(responce,trackType,trackData,redirectUrl){
    console.log(responce);
	if (responce === 0){
        var aloomaPageData = {};
        trackData.token = 'gBsWnjXdjn';
        aloomaPageData.event = trackType;
        aloomaPageData.properties = trackData;

        var pixel_img = document.createElement("img");
        pixel_img.setAttribute("src", window.location.origin + "/jssdk/track/pixel.php?data="+encodeURIComponent(b64EncodeUnicode(JSON.stringify(aloomaPageData))));
        pixel_img.setAttribute("height", "1");
        pixel_img.setAttribute("width", "1");
        pixel_img.setAttribute("alt", "vpnMentor");
        document.body.appendChild(pixel_img);

        if (redirectUrl !== undefined) {
            window.location = redirectUrl;
        }
    }
}

var TrackingQueryString = function () {

	// This function is anonymous, is executed immediately and
	// the return value is assigned to QueryString!
	var query_string = {};
	var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
	var vars = query.split("&");
	for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
		var pair = vars[i].split("=");
			// If first entry with this name
		if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "undefined") {
		query_string[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(pair[1]));
		//console.log(query_string[pair[0]]);
			// If second entry with this name
		} else if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "string") {
		var arr = [ query_string[pair[0]],decodeURIComponent(pair[1]) ];
		query_string[pair[0]] = arr;
			// If third or later entry with this name
		} else {
		query_string[pair[0]].push(decodeURIComponent(pair[1]));
		}
	}
	return query_string;
	} ();

function b64EncodeUnicode(str) {
    // first we use encodeURIComponent to get percent-encoded UTF-8,
    // then we convert the percent encodings into raw bytes which
    // can be fed into btoa.
    return btoa(encodeURIComponent(str).replace(/%([0-9A-F]{2})/g,
        function toSolidBytes(match, p1) {
            return String.fromCharCode('0x' + p1);
    }));
}

  <script>
   var xhr = null;

	if (typeof setCookie === 'undefined') {
    function setCookie(c_name, value, exdays) {
        var exdate = new Date();
        if ( c_name == 'BC' ) {
            if ( value == "undefined") {
                value = true;
            }
            exdate.setTime(exdate.getTime() + exdays*60000);
        } else {
            exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
        }
        var domainSplit = window.location.hostname.split('.');
        var domain = '.'+domainSplit[1]+'.'+domainSplit[2];
        var c_value = escape(value) + ((exdays == null) ? ";path=/" : ";path=/; expires=" + exdate.toUTCString());
        document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value+";domain="+domain;
    }
}
if (typeof getCookie === "undefined") {
    function getCookie(name) {
        var value = "; " + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
        if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
    }
}

var QueryString = function() {
    // This function is anonymous, is executed immediately and
    // the return value is assigned to QueryString!
    var query_string = {};
    var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
    var vars = query.split("&");
    for (var i = 0; i < vars.length; i++) {
        var pair = vars[i].split("=");
        // If first entry with this name
        if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "undefined") {
            query_string[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(pair[1]));
            // If second entry with this name
        } else if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "string") {
            var arr = [query_string[pair[0]], decodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(pair[1]))];
            query_string[pair[0]] = arr;
            // If third or later entry with this name
        } else {
            query_string[pair[0]].push(decodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(pair[1])));
        }
    }
    return query_string;
}();



function addAdwords(value) {
    setCookie('gclid', value, 30);
}

// Add Brand Adv
function addBc(value) {
    var bcContent = "";

    if (Array.isArray(value)){
        bcContent = value[1];
    } else {
        bcContent = value;
    }

    if (bcContent == 'true') {
        setCookie('BC', bcContent, 15);
    }
}


function addYandex(value) {
    setCookie('yclid', value, 30);
}

function addMScode(value) {
    setCookie('msclkid', value, 30);
}

function addTaboolaCode(value) {
    setCookie('tblcid', value, 30);
}

function addAddParams(campaign, adgroup, keyword) {
    setCookie('advParams', campaign + '_' + adgroup + '_' + keyword, 30);
}

if (window.location.search.indexOf('gclid') > -1) {
    addAdwords(QueryString.gclid);
}
if (window.location.search.indexOf('bc') > -1) {
    addBc(QueryString.bc);
}
if (window.location.search.indexOf('yclid') > -1) {
    addYandex(QueryString.yclid);
}
if (window.location.search.indexOf('msclkid') > -1) {
    addMScode(QueryString.msclkid);
}
if (window.location.search.indexOf('tblcid') > -1) {
    addTaboolaCode(QueryString.tblcid);
}
if (window.location.search.indexOf('campaign') > -1) {
    var campaign = 'ca',
        adgroup = 'ad',
        keyword = 'kw';
    if (window.location.search.indexOf('campaign') > -1) {
        campaign = campaign + QueryString.campaign;
    }
    if (window.location.search.indexOf('adgroup') > -1) {
        adgroup = adgroup + QueryString.adgroup;
    }
    if (window.location.search.indexOf('keyword') > -1) {
        keyword = keyword + QueryString.keyword;
    }
    addAddParams(campaign, adgroup, keyword);
}

if (window.location.search.indexOf('gclid') > -1 || window.location.search.indexOf('yclid') > -1 || window.location.search.indexOf('campaign') > -1 || window.location.search.indexOf('msclkid') > -1 || window.location.search.indexOf('tblcid') > -1 || window.location.search.indexOf('UTM_Source') > -1) {
    var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
    setCookie('FullAdvParams', query, 30);
}


    if (typeof lazyLoadImages != 'function') {
        var lazyLoadImages = function (scroll) {

            var size = scroll ? 2 : 1;

            [].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('img[data-src],source[data-srcset]'), function (img) { //Lazy loading during scroll
                if ((Math.abs(img.getBoundingClientRect().top) <= (window.innerHeight * size) && img.getBoundingClientRect().top > 0 && !img.hasAttribute('src') && !img.hasAttribute('srcset'))) { //Element is 2 pages away from view port
                    // if ( "picture" === img.tagName.toLowerCase() ) {
                    //     var sources = img.querySelectorAll('source');
                    //     for (var N=0; N < sources.length; N++) {
                    //         sources[N].setAttribute('srcset', sources[N].getAttribute('data-srcset'));
                    //         sources[N].removeAttribute('data-srcset');
                    //     }
                    //     img.classList.remove("picture-lazy");
                    //}
                    // } else {
                    if (img.hasAttribute('data-src')) {
                        img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-src'));
                    }
                    if (img.hasAttribute('data-srcset')) {
                        img.setAttribute('srcset', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
                    }

                    img.onload = function () {
                        img.removeAttribute('data-src');
                        img.removeAttribute('data-srcset');

                        if (img.hasAttribute('data-with-lazy-wrap')) {
                            img.removeAttribute('data-with-lazy-wrap');
                            $(img).closest(".img-lazy-wrap").removeClass("img-lazy-wrap").addClass("img-lazy-wrap--loaded");
                        }
                    };
                } else if (img.parentNode.getAttribute('class') == 'cssload-thecube loader') {
                    img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-src'));
                    img.onload = function () {
                        img.removeAttribute('data-src');
                    };
                }
            });
        }

        $(document).ready(function () {
            lazyLoadImages();

            // Fix for Tools on the big screens without scroll: bottom avatars does not loading as page is fit to the screen size
            if (window.outerHeight < $("body").height() + 250) {
                setTimeout(lazyLoadImages, 1500);
            }
        });

    }

    if (typeof loadImages != 'function') {
        var loadImages = function (target) {//load image on container on call
            [].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll(target + ' img[data-src]'), function (img) {
                if (!img.hasAttribute('src')) {
                    img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-src'));
                    if (img.hasAttribute('data-srcset')) {
                        img.setAttribute('srcset', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
                    }
                    img.onload = function () {
                        img.removeAttribute('data-src');
                        img.removeAttribute('data-srcset');
                        if (img.hasAttribute('data-with-lazy-wrap')) {
                            img.removeAttribute('data-with-lazy-wrap');
                            $(img).closest(".img-lazy-wrap").removeClass("img-lazy-wrap").addClass("img-lazy-wrap--loaded");
                        }
                    };
                }
            });
        }
    }

	    if (typeof delayedLazyLoadImages != 'function') {
        var delayedLazyLoadImages = function () {
            [].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('img[data-src]'), function (img) {
                if (img.getBoundingClientRect().top == 0 && !img.hasAttribute('src')) { // Images with no definite positioning on screen due to being hidden, will load after 5 sec of document load.
                    img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-src'));
                    img.onload = function () {
                        img.removeAttribute('data-src');
                    };
                }
            });
        }

        setTimeout(function () {
            delayedLazyLoadImages()
        }, 5000);
    }
	
    $(document).on("scroll", function () {
        lazyLoadImages(true)
    });

    $(function () {// START OF DOCUMENT READY

		
		
        if (xhrs != null) {
            xhrs.abort();
        }

		
    }); // END OF DOCUMENT READY

    // @TODO : it is BING init!!! are you kidding me??? Remove this in future
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
